< text>
I purchased my mattress from Mattress Firm a little over a year ago (original review below) and I wanted to upgrade my pillows. I initial bought some cheap pillows off of Amazon when I purchased my bed and now a year later and the pillows are lumpy and causing me some discomfort in my neck. I decided it was time to invest in some good quality pillows, so I reached out to Mesfin who was still with the company (thank God!) and he advised me that I should come into the store during their Memorial Day Sale to test out some options.

Mesfin educated me on the importance of a good pillow. He had me test out several pillows, on the exact make and model of the bed that I initial purchased from Mattress Firm, so that I could see how the pillow felt on top of my actual bed! Who would have thought that, that was a thing?!! Makes sense though when you think about it.

I purchased 2 great pillows. I'm so glad that I did not purchase the pillows online and that I took the time to come into the store. I am even more thankful that Mesfin helped me with something so trival as picking out pillows.

Once again, I've had a great experience with Mattress Firm & Mesfin. I will be going back for all my future mattress and of course pillow needs!

Review as of 2/22/18

As a woman I am always leery of being taken advantage of when it comes to things such as getting any work done on my vehicle, or in this case buying a brand-new mattress.  I went to Mattress Firm to do some preliminary research before I made a purchase. I was greeted by the store manager, Mesfin, who was welcoming and personable. He took me around the show room and educated me on each mattress. He was extremely knowledgeable about their selection of mattresses and was very patient with me. I tested each one out and by process of elimination, he helped me find the perfect mattress for me. He took his time and answered all my questions, he really exceeded all my expectations. When I was finally ready to make my purchase 2 weeks later, he even helped me get financing!  Overall, I had a pleasant experience, Mesfin took the nervousness and anxiety out of making such a huge purchase.<//text>

First, they recently tried to refuse replacing a grip even though they put on the wrong one.  They only agreed once they realized the grip was incorrectly put on anyways.  This was for a brand new club, so I guess there margin was not enough on the club itself.  They tried blaming me for the mistake.

Second, I brought in a pair of leaking shoes, still under warranty, and a different employee tried to argue that I had simply played too many rounds.  Number of rounds do not change the 2 year warranty policy, so not really sure why they were arguing.  I eventually received replaced shoes, but don't understand the argument.

Third, I have tied three times in the last month to get fitted for new irons.  I have money burning my pockets, but unfortunately, no one seems to have the time to help.  Either folks are taking breaks or are just too busy.  Ok, I see a bunch of folks doing nothing, or at least not revenue enhancing activities, yet they cannot find the time to fit me with new irons.  Hmm, don't get that either!

There are a few really good employees that work there, but this is no longer the establishment it once was.  I would recommend just finding what you want at the store and order it online.  You will probably get a better price.  Plus some of the online sites are even offering trial periods.

I am sad to write this review given the many years I enjoyed spending hours at Golf Mart.  The business approach worked because I have bought all my clubs there for the last 20 years.  No more!!!  Hopefully, management realizes what is happening soon before they lose too much business.

Your former customer</Review><Pictures>None<//Pictures><resp>None<//resp>< Gmap_id>

<time>1544570207702<//time><Rating>5</Rating>< review>
I arrived hungry and ready. Inside a small cozy spot with a warm welcoming homey feel, grandmas kitchen. My first time here, and the staff was pleasant in explaining the different types of dishes.

I ordered a freshly made watermelon drink to start, it arrives quickly and it was perfectly refreshing - not too sweet.

I order the Mole Neigro "Dark Mole", and to my delight it was the perfect spicy note. I was making yummy sounds.... it was that good. It comes with freshly made tortillas, a side of rice, and a salsa cup for additional heat, if needed. My tongue and lips are buzzing with the heat, but I can't stop eating. Sipping my watermelon drink with this delicious mole, I am in a very happy food place right now.

This place might look like a hole-in-the-wall, but when I close my eyes while enjoying the food - I am in my grandmas. I see myself dangerously visiting this awesome restaurant multiple times a month.

I highly recommend everyone to give this Restaurant a chance,  you will not be disappointed.  Cash only place!</review>

<Review>I've been banking with SESLOC for 10+ years, and had excellent service. We've opened multiple accounts, including several for our kids, made many wire transfers & inter-account transfers, no problems.

When it comes down to it, the biggest reason to choose a local credit union is this: SESLOC isn't trying to suck your money out and funnel it to corporate shareholders like major commercial banks; they're locally run, and they're a credit union, meaning that *you* are the shareholders. I honestly don't understand the appeal of a commercial bank, and I'm somewhat baffled by the number of Americans that use Chase, Wells Fargo, etc. etc. etc.

<Rating>5<//Rating>< Review>
Hi, I'm Tim. I'm a Retired General Contractor, and I also used to own and operate my own landscape company. And as such, I am pretty picky my home, and how it looks. (The Pictures I Provided Speak For Them Selves, my wife and I do all our own work on our home from painting, laying pavers to landscaping). So due to that, I am generally reluctant to let anyone else work on my home, as I want it to be done right. So when my wife suggested we start looking at artificial turf to replace our beautiful Marathon Sod Yard, due to the severe drought here in So Cal, I was quite hesitant to look at, and trust anyone In that business. As I have seen a lot of really fake looking yards in out neighborhood. And I have heard numerous horror stories of poor installs/workmanship, poor quality turf products, smelly turf due to pets etc. (I have 5 dogs) So I did my research, and set up 5 interviews/quotes with what I considered to be the best 5 prospects based on my research. After all the interviews, I chose to go with Pro Lawn, as Mike Clark their owner was by far the most professional of them all. Let me explain what I mean. 1. He was able to answer all my questions and concerns with facts. (not the other guys, I got a lot of maybes, and I'll have too ask someone else) 2. He was able to show me samples of all the products when he came to the appointment. He was prepared. (the others did not have complete samples) 3. I was able to discuss my whole plan with him, and get his feed back, as not only was he the owner, but he was very experienced in all phases of this type of construction. As he get's his hands dirty doing the work as well. (the other guys were sales people with nothing but a quote, and a desire to get a signed deal that day) 4. We only had 900 sq. feet to do. The other company's said it would take anywhere from 2 to 5 days, depending on how many guys they could send. Mike said they would be done in one day. He would have a four man crew coming. 5. Mike was never pushy in any way. He was very respectful of me and my home and what we were trying to accomplish. So based on those facts, who would you choose??? A no brainer, right. So yes, we choose Pro Lawn. Now I must admit, I was still a little apprehensive regarding the actual install, as I'm letting a group of strangers work on my home. But on the day of the install when the Pro Lawn crew showed up, and I met the foreman and his crew, all my doubts went away. First they were on time. They were dressed professionally for the task at hand. They had all the tool's and materials with them to do the job. They reviewed everything they were going to do and why, and asked for my input. And during the procedure, keep me in the loop 100%. There were no surprises. They were like military operation in their approach. No wasted energy or time. You could tell they really knew what they were doing. Everything they did from the sod removal to the install of the turf was well planned. No guess work. And they really took pride in how and what they were doing. They wanted us to like the results of their craft. They were very impressive to watch. We were amazed to say the least. That was in 2014. Here we are 4 years later, and our lawn still looks amazing. (With 5 Dogs Mind You) No issues. I took these pic's today, 3/3/2018. And yes, I would do it again in a heart beat. Thanks' to  Mike and his amazing team, my home looks amazing. I just got invited to be in the parade of gardens in Clairmont. I have people stop by all the time and take pictures and ask how we take care of the turf. I tell them I only use a blower. Hee Hee. Anyway, I could go on for ever about my wonderful experience. But I think you get the point. We are one happy customer. Tim & Leesa</Review>

<user>112202848636781237224< /user>< name>
Gratitude Attracts Blessings - Sam</name>
< date>
1601009090638</date>
<rating>3< /rating>< text>
Food ‚≠ê‚≠ê‚≠ê‚≠ê‚≠ê Service ‚≠ê‚≠ê‚≠ê
Personal Touch ‚≠ê‚≠ê

Restaurants are like love affairs. It doesn't have to be perfect, but some things will make it last.

We came from a far to visit this restaurant. We waited about 40 minutes for a table. Met Fadi, the Jordanian entrepreneur who owns the restaurant. Very pleasant.

The food was absolutely delicious. The sauces were just perfectly done, not overly creamy, just the right consistency. The food combinations were awesome.

The server didn't recommend any appetizers. Went from drinks to main course. When asked about the Ravioli special vs. the seafood pasta, he said he liked both but couldn't recommend one over the other. So I ordered both. Though the owner knew we came from a far and it was to celebrate a birthday, there was no effort to make the birthday girl's evening special.

The server only visited the table just once since the order. The owner didn't visit any tables while we were there.

We would have ordered dessert and wine had the service was better. This is where the relationship part come in. We would have gladly spent a lot more money, but went elsewhere for dessert and wine.

There was a table of 4 next to us who just had water, no dessert, but was googling where to go from there. Missed opportunity.

There are many great restaurants in Carmel. We come to Carmel often. We come for that special Carmel experience and service. I hope Fadi realizes that it's a privilege to have customers, not a privilege to eat at his restaurant. Make the customers feel amazing and they will return even if the food missed a beat that day or on that dish.

Great potential at this location and at this restaurant. Keep the kitchen staff, but change the attitude, spend more time taking care of your customers. Get to know them. They will come back. They will spend more money per check. They will be more forgiving.< /text>

< text>
The food is amazing here. The host, waiters, bussers and cooks all worked amazing together last night as a team. The restaurant was so busy and the wait was long. I highly recommend making reservations in advance... Just don't be too upset when your reservation becomes delayed because a large group doesn't want to finish their wine. I got to give it to this restaurant last night. I made reservations for 8 pm last night.. we probably were seated around 8:30pm maybe later it was definitely crowded. The staff all were wearing masks perfectly like you would hope. Tables are spaced apart. Only con is they only have one restroom... But what can you do.

I had the calamari for an appetizer and yellow curry for dinner. My spouse has the Greek burger with salad. Both were mouth watering. I don't normally like calamari but it was a steak and cooked to perfection.
This place has a wonderful romantic atmosphere and is dog and family friendly. If you are willing to wait for a seat on the deck I think it is worth it.
Thank you staff for our best night in Carmel. A great way to end a small vacation post covid.</text>

Aaron Elliott< /user_name>
< date>
1567440366182</date>
<Rate>1<//Rate>< Review>
I was expecting at least a solid 3 in dining experience, based on the overall 4.6 rating (restaurant ratings in and around Monterey seem to be artificially inflated, for some reason).

The servers were friendly, but did forget to put our appetizer order in. We got the chicken pesto pasta and the beef stroganoff. Both dishes were severely lacking in meat portions, so we ended up paying about $22 - $24 for a bowl of noodles. The meals were relatively bland and tasteless. I think this restaurant uses its location, rather than food quality, to attract customers.

The chicken pesto pasta was greasy and oily for some reason. The chicken was not great.

The beef stroganoff was the saddest thing we received. There were 5 tiny pieces of beef in a huge bowl of noodles. They advertised mushrooms in this recipe, but we found no mushrooms in the bowl. They advertise this as Russian beef stroganoff. What they neglect to mention is this is the wartime rationed meat version of Russian beef stroganoff.

Overall, we were extremely disappointed and will not be back. I don't know what's up with the 5 star reviews, but we certainly did not have a great experience. I believe just about any restaurant in the Barnyard shopping center is superior, so I recommend you go there instead.< /Review>

< Text>
Pretty place for sure, but without being treated right, it's hard to appreciate it.

We were seated by an uncomfortable corner of the patio right next to where the waiters constantly walk past. That was okay, since we could've chosen to change. Once our waiter appeared, he asks us 3 questions stereotyping us, mechanically and unthinkingly. After his "revealing questions", it is soon exposed within seconds of being seated that we are vegetarians. Again, too soon and too mechanically, he gives us 3 quick options that are the only ones available to us and to let him know. Waiter quickly exits the scene.

We wonder for a few minutes on what that was and decide that this is not the experience we want to give our money for. And thus we make our exit too.< /Text>

<user_id>110719912551766631522< /user_id><GmapID>0x808de615ab8d5b45:0x39edb77f78473005<//GmapID>< date>

< Review>
Average for the area but the area is very very good.

Atmosphere- 4 stars. Even though the rooftop deck in on the street, traffic sounds were low and trees in the area aw well as the building itself create a relaxing atmosphere. Dog friendly even though you have to walk through he restaurant to get to the deck.

Food. 3.5 stars.   The food was good.  We had Chicken Pesto Pasta.  The pasta was cooked perfectly and the chicken was tender.  The pesto cream sauce was rich but not oily.    They let us split the plate which was about perfect for lunch.

Service: 0 stars.  Servers were attentive and kind but I had an issue with my glass of wine.  I had an expensive glass of nice wine which I was nursing through dinner and had only had a couple of sips.

Near the end of dinner, a gust of wind flipped the table cloth up spilling my mostly full glass of wine.  I got a servers attention and told him what had happened and asked for some new napkins since ours were drenched in wine.  They  mopped up the wine with  the napkins but left a damp table and    didn't come back with new napkins.  They also didn't offer to comp or top off my glass.  That was a major fail.</Review>
